<!--SS_BEGIN_SNIPPET(fragment8,header)-->				<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript" src="/prod_ext/fragments/bps_font_size/scripts/textsizer.js"></script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
	function activateFontSize()
	{
		//alert('CookiFS: '+getCookieFontSize());
		var fontSize = getCookieFontSize();
		
		if(fontSize != "doNotResize"){
			setFontSize('body', (fontSize*1));
		}
	}
	window.onload=activateFontSize;
</script>

<!--SS_BEGIN_SNIPPET(region1_element6,header)-->
				<script type="text/javascript">
	var lastSelectedLetter = "A";
	
	function switchLetters(selectedLetter)
	{
		//clean up the last selected divs - top A-Z browse
		var lastSelectedLetterDiv=document.getElementById(lastSelectedLetter);
		lastSelectedLetterDiv.className = "atoz";

		//clean up the last selected divs - bottom A-Z browse
		var lastSelectedLetterDivBottom=document.getElementById(lastSelectedLetter + "-bottom");
		lastSelectedLetterDivBottom.className = "atoz";
		
		//clean up the last selected divs - bigletter
		var lastSelectedBigLetterDiv=document.getElementById("bigLetter");
		lastSelectedBigLetterDiv.innerHTML = selectedLetter;
		
		lastSelectedLetter = selectedLetter;

		//turn on new selected divs - top A-Z Browse
		var selectedLetterDiv=document.getElementById(selectedLetter);
		selectedLetterDiv.className= "atoz_selected";
		
		//turn on new selected divs - bottom A-Z Browse
		var selectedLetterDivBottom=document.getElementById(selectedLetter + "-bottom");
		selectedLetterDivBottom.className= "atoz_selected";
		
		//clean up the last selected divs and show new - the search results
		showHideSearchResultRows(selectedLetter)

	}
	
	//this method finds all the rows in the results div and show/hides the non-title ones
	function showHideSearchResultRows(letter){
		var mainDiv = document.getElementById("mainDiv")
		var resultRows=mainDiv.getElementsByTagName("tr");
		for(var i = 0; i<resultRows.length; i++){
			if(resultRows[i].className != "titlebar"){
				if(resultRows[i].getAttribute("name") == letter + "-resultRow"){
					resultRows[i].style.display = "";
				}else{
					resultRows[i].style.display = "none";
				}
			}
		}

	}
	
</script>
			<!--SS_END_SNIPPET(region1_element6,header)-->

<!--SS_BEGIN_SNIPPET(region1_element7,header)-->
				<script type="text/javascript">

	var lastHighlighted="";

	
	
	function showHideBrowse(groupAValue)
	{
		var mainTable = document.getElementById("mainTable");
		var resultRows=mainTable.getElementsByTagName("tr");
		for(var i = 0; i<resultRows.length; i++){
		
			//go through all the rows and if they are not headers or the main rows show/hide them
			if(resultRows[i].className != "titlebar" && resultRows[i].getAttribute("name") != "MainRows"){
				if(resultRows[i].getAttribute("name").indexOf(groupAValue+"-", 0) == 0){
					//when grouped on 2 metadata fields the name has "-SubHeading", but when grouped on only one it has "--" instead
					if(resultRows[i].style.display == "none" && 
						(resultRows[i].getAttribute("name").indexOf("-SubHeading", 0) > 0 || 
						 resultRows[i].getAttribute("name").indexOf("--", 0) > 0)){
						resultRows[i].style.display = "";
						
					}else{
						resultRows[i].style.display = "none";
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		//set minuses to pluses
		var imagesArray = document.getElementsByTagName("img");
		for(var i = 0; i<imagesArray.length; i++){
			if(imagesArray[i].id.indexOf(groupAValue) > -1 && imagesArray[i].id.indexOf(groupAValue+"-img") == -1){
				imagesArray[i].src=imagesArray[i].src.replace(/_close/, "_open");
			}
		}		
		
		changeLookMain(groupAValue);
	}
	
	function showHideSubBrowse(groupAValue, groupBValue)
	{
		var mainTable = document.getElementById("mainTable");
		var resultRows=mainTable.getElementsByTagName("tr");
		for(var i = 0; i<resultRows.length; i++){
		
			//go through all the rows and if they are not headers or the main rows show/hide them
			if(resultRows[i].className != "titlebar" && resultRows[i].getAttribute("name") != "MainRows"){
				if(resultRows[i].getAttribute("name") == groupAValue + "-" + groupBValue + "-Data"){
					if(resultRows[i].style.display == "none"){
						resultRows[i].style.display = "";
					}else{
						resultRows[i].style.display = "none";
					}
				}
			}
		}
		

		changeLookSub(groupAValue, groupBValue);
	}

	
	function changeLookMain(rowName){

		if(lastHighlighted != ""){
			var cellLast1 = document.getElementById(lastHighlighted + "-1");
			cellLast1.className="highlight_row_gray";
		}

		var cell1 = document.getElementById(rowName + "-1");
		cell1.className="highlight_row";
		
		var imgElement = document.getElementById(rowName + "-img");
		if(imgElement.src.indexOf("_close") > 0){
			imgElement.src=imgElement.src.replace(/_close/, "_open");
		}else if(imgElement.src.indexOf("_open") > 0){
			imgElement.src=imgElement.src.replace(/_open/, "_close");
		}
		
		lastHighlighted = rowName;
	}
	
		
	function changeLookSub(rowNameA, rowNameB){
		
		var imgElement = document.getElementById(rowNameA + "-" + rowNameB + "-SubHeading-img");
		if(imgElement.src.indexOf("_close") > 0){
			imgElement.src=imgElement.src.replace(/_close/, "_open");
		}else if(imgElement.src.indexOf("_open") > 0){
			imgElement.src=imgElement.src.replace(/_open/, "_close");
		}

	}
	
</script>
			<!--SS_END_SNIPPET(region1_element7,header)-->

<script type="text/javascript">
/* Set the top nav to redirect appropriately */
function loginRedirect() {     
    var defaultLink = jQuery('select#selLogin').val();
    jQuery('select#selLogin').click(function() {
        redirectLink = jQuery(this).val();  
        // Only redirect if a value is set
        if (redirectLink != defaultLink) {
            window.location = redirectLink;
        }
    });
}   
var loginButton = jQuery('#loginButton');
function showLoginOptions() {
    loginButton.parent().toggleClass('hideSubMenu');
}

jQuery(document).ready(function() {
    loginButton.click(showLoginOptions);        

});

</script>
